# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 08:23:08.116498

### Base Program

```py
def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```

## Test Case 10

### Modified Program

```py

def maxDistToClosest(seats):
    n = len(seats)
    maxDist = 0
    lastPerson = -1

    for i in range(n):
        if seats[i] == 1:
            if lastPerson == -1:
                maxDist = i
            else:
                maxDist = max(maxDist, (i - lastPerson) // 2)
            lastPerson = i

    maxDist = max(maxDist, n - 1 - lastPerson)
    return maxDist


```
